<script type="application/javascript">

  $q('html').click(function() {
    $q('.topBarFloatingNotifications').hide();    $q('.topBarFloatingUserSettings').hide();
    $q('.topBarFloatingInbox').hide();
  });

  function toggleInbox(event) {
    $q('.topBarFloatingNotifications').hide();    $q('.topBarFloatingUserSettings').hide();
    $q('.topBarFloatingInbox').toggle();
    event.stopPropagation();
  }

  function toggleUserSettings(event) {
    $q('.topBarFloatingInbox').hide();
    $q('.topBarFloatingNotifications').hide();
    $q('.topBarFloatingUserSettings').toggle();
    $q('#usernameArrow').toggleClass('partiallyHidden');
    event.stopPropagation();
  }

  function logout() {
    $q('#logoutForm').submit();
  }

    function toggleNotifications(event) {
    $q('.topBarFloatingInbox').hide();
    $q('.topBarFloatingUserSettings').hide();
    $q('.topBarFloatingNotifications').toggle();
    event.stopPropagation();

    $q.ajax({
      url: "/?noticesRead",
      context: document.body,
      success: function(){
        if(!$q('#notificationsCount').hasClass('noNotifications')) {
          $q('#notificationsCount').addClass('noNotifications');
          $q('#notificationsCount').text(0);
        }
      }
    });
  }
  </script>

<script type="application/javascript">
	$q('.login').click(function() {
		$q('#signUpDialog').hide();
		$q('#loginDialog').show();
	})
	$q('#loginDialog').click(function(){
		$q('#loginDialog').hide();
	})
	$q('.closeButton').click(function(){
		$q('#loginDialog').hide();
		$q('#signUpDialog').hide();
	})
	$q('.loginDialogBox').click(function(event){
		event.stopPropagation();
	})
	$q('.signUpDialogBox').click(function(event){
		event.stopPropagation();
	})

	$q('#signUpDialog').click(function(){
		$q('#signUpDialog').hide();
	})

	$q('.signup').click(function() {
    $q.getScript( "https://www.google.com/recaptcha/api.js", function( data, textStatus, jqxhr ) {
    });

		$q('#loginDialog').hide();
		$q('#signUpDialog').show();
	})


</script>

	<script type="application/javascript">
		$q('.tzTimestamp').each(function(index, obj) {
			var timestampVal = obj.innerHTML;
			var date = new Date(timestampVal*1000);
      $q(obj).html(moment(date).format("HH:mm"))
		});

	<script>
		$q(document).ready(function()
		{
			var unFilter = $q('<img title="Show all matches" style="cursor:pointer;margin-top:5px;margin-right:5px;float:right" src="http://static.hltv.org//images/filterActive.png">');
			var filter = $q('<img title="Only show top matches" style="cursor:pointer;text-align:-20%;margin-top:5px;margin-right:5px;float:right" src="http://static.hltv.org//images/filterUnactive.png">');

			var resUnFilter = $q('<img title="Show all matches" style="cursor:pointer;margin-top:5px;margin-right:5px;float:right" src="http://static.hltv.org//images/filterActive.png">');
			var resFilter = $q('<img title="Only show top matches" style="cursor:pointer;text-align:-20%;margin-top:5px;margin-right:5px;float:right" src="http://static.hltv.org//images/filterUnactive.png">');


			unFilter.click(function () {
				unFilter.detach();
				resUnFilter.detach();
				$q('.notStarred').show();
				$q('.originallyHidden').hide();
				$q('#matchFilter').append(filter)
				$q('#resFilter').append(resFilter)
				Cookies.set('filterMatches', '0', {expires: 9999});
			});

			filter.click(function () {
				filter.detach();
				resFilter.detach();
				$q('.notStarred').hide();
				$q('.starred').show();
				$q('#matchFilter').append(unFilter)
				$q('#resFilter').append(resUnFilter)
				Cookies.set('filterMatches', '1', {expires: 9999});
			});

			if (Cookies.get("filterMatches") == 1) {
				$q('#matchFilter').append(unFilter)
				$q('#resFilter').append(resUnFilter)
				$q('.notStarred').hide();
				$q('.starred').show();
			} else {
				$q('#matchFilter').append(filter)
				$q('#resFilter').append(resFilter)
				$q('.notStarred').show();
				$q('.originallyHidden').hide();
			}

			//res

			resUnFilter.click(function () {
				resUnFilter.detach();
				unFilter.detach();
				$q('.notStarred').show();
				$q('.originallyHidden').hide();
				$q('#resFilter').append(resFilter)
				$q('#matchFilter').append(filter)
				Cookies.set('filterMatches', '0', {expires: 9999});
			});

			resFilter.click(function () {
				resFilter.detach();
				filter.detach();
				$q('.notStarred').hide();
				$q('.starred').show();
				$q('#resFilter').append(resUnFilter)
				$q('#matchFilter').append(unFilter)
				Cookies.set('filterMatches', '1', {expires: 9999});
			});

			if (Cookies.get("filterMatches") == 1) {
				$q('#resFilter').append(resUnFilter)
				$q('#matchFilter').append(unFilter)
				$q('.notStarred').hide();
				$q('.starred').show();
			} else {
				$q('#resFilter').append(resFilter)
				$q('#matchFilter').append(filter)
				$q('.notStarred').show();
				$q('.originallyHidden').hide();
			}
		})
	</script>

    allFragMatrix.id = 'matrix_allfrags';
    allFragMatrix.tabGroup = 'matrixTabGroup';
    allFragMatrix.isSelected = false;
    allFragMatrix.defaultForParent = true;
    allFragMatrix.dataUrl = '/?pageid=113&matchid=' + 2308872 +'&killMatrix=1&clean=1';

    links.push(allFragMatrix)


    var entryFragMatrix = {};
    entryFragMatrix.parent = 'matrix_link';
    entryFragMatrix.id = 'matrix_entryfrags';
    entryFragMatrix.tabGroup = 'matrixTabGroup';
    entryFragMatrix.isSelected = false;
    entryFragMatrix.defaultForParent = false;
    entryFragMatrix.dataUrl = '/?pageid=113&matchid=' + 2308872 +'&killMatrix=1&entry=1&clean=1';
    entryFragMatrix.title = 'Opening kill matrix';
    links.push(entryFragMatrix)


    $q(function () {
      $q('.statsNav').click(function (event) {
        var found = false;
        links.forEach(function (link) {
          if (event.target.id == link.id) {
            setSelected(link)
            found = true
          }
        });
        if (!found) {
          links.forEach(function (link) {
            if (event.target.id == link.parent && link.defaultForParent) {
              setSelected(link)
            }
          });
        }
      })
    });

    function setSelected(link) {
      unselect(currentlySelected)
      showTabGroup(link.tabGroup)
      colorBlack(link.parent)
      colorBlack(link.id)
      currentlySelected = link
      loadData(link)
    }

    function setTitle(title) {
      $q('#statsTitle').html(title)
    }

    function loadData(link) {
      $q.ajax({
        type: 'GET',
        url: link.dataUrl,
        success: function (data) {
          setTitle(link.title)
          $q("#statsContainer").html(data);
        }
      })
    }

    function showTabGroup(id) {
      $q('#' + id).show();
    }

    function hideTabGroup(id) {
      $q('#' + id).hide();
    }

    function unselect(link) {
      colorBlue(link.parent)
      colorBlue(link.id)
      hideTabGroup(link.tabGroup)
    }

    function colorBlack(id) {
      $q('#' + id).css('color', 'black')
    }

    function colorBlue(id) {
      $q('#' + id).css('color', '#0269D2')
    }

    $q('.statsNav').css('color', '#0269D2')
    $q('.statsNav').css('cursor', 'pointer')
    hideTabGroup('matrixTabGroup')
    hideTabGroup('mapsTabGroup')

    currentlySelected = allMapsLink
    setSelected(allMapsLink);
  </script>

<script type="application/javascript">
  $q('.manofthematchbutton').click(function () {
    $q(this).addClass('voted');
    $q.ajax({
      url: "/?pageid=113&clean=1&matchid=2308872&momvote=1&playerid=" + this.id,
      context: document.body,
      success: function (data) {
        var json = $q.parseJSON(data);
        $q.each(json, function(i, item) {
          $q('#'+i +'.manofthematchbutton').html(item+'%')
        });
        $q('.manofthematchbutton:not(.voted)').each(function (item) {
          $q(this).css({ opacity: 0.7, cursor: 'default' });
        })
        $q('.manofthematchbutton.voted').each(function (item) {
          $q(this).css({cursor: 'default' });
        })
      }
    });
  });
  $q('.manofthematchvotedbutton').each(function (item) {
    $q(this).css({ opacity: 0.7, cursor: 'default' });
  })
  $q('.manofthematchbuttonhighlight').each(function (item) {
    $q(this).css({ cursor: 'default' });
  })


</script>
